< Text>
What an amazing placed filled with amazing people! We were just in Palm Springs for a week, and we entertained friends at our home multiple times throughout our stay there, and On the Mark was our reliable source for everything but mostly their beautiful charcuterie spreads. They are kind, helpful, knowledgable, and their ingredients are so fresh that we returned 4 of our 7 nights for dinner ingredients, etc. This is exactly what our little city needed, and they were so sweet to accommodate us with a one hour notice for a spread. I can't recommend this place more, and look forward to hosting more of their goodies!<//Text>

< review>
Incredible hole on the wall here. Their catering is incredible but also come in to grab a delicious sandwich and try various very delicious cheeses, spread, mustards etc.

ALSO: TRY THEIR EXOTIC CHOCALATES!! Batch specific, curated chocolates... unbelievable

Their sandwiches use bread baked that am which really compliment the extreme quality ingredients they use to build your sandwich. I had the Wisconsin on fresh baked, moist sour dough with amazing carmelized dark crust... must try, the cheese and meats are out of this world!
As far as catering goes, the presentation is on a board that shows extremely well and of course the foods are on a completely nother level... TRY IT!</review>

< Review>
I've been a renter at ExtraSpace for about 7 months and the staff (Adrian & Frank) at the Grand Terrace location have always done everything possible to assure I am satisfied always.

A week ago I was moving a Bicycle from the storage unit and discovered I didnt have the tools required to break parts of the bike down. I had resolved to leave the bike in Grand Terrace until my next visit that's when Frank asked if he could be of assistance. I told him my plight and he said he just might have the tools in his truck that would do the job. He had the tools and 15 years experience as an AirForce Mechanic that made quick work of the task.

When you want a good storage location with great people that run the establishment with a fantastic approach to customer service, think ExtraSpace Storage Grand Terrace, Ca.<//Review>

< review>
Out of all the places I've been to for my general car maintenance, this place takes the top.  Fair prices, decent wait times, and friendly staff that aren't as pushy on services as most other places.  They have found things on my cars over the years that I miss and always have a recommendation if it's something they can fix.

They even gave me a few pointers on the safest way to tighten the drain plug on the oil pan on my civic, after I had stripped the previous pan when I replaced the gasket on it and ended up buying a new pan since I didn't want to tap the plug.  Why do I go to them for oil changes if I can change an oil pan?  Because I don't like going under my car and these guys find stuff I miss .  Plus, I don't feel like having bottles of every fluid for both of my cars in the garage.

The one time they had oil spill a little underneath the car, they cleaned up everything pretty well.  I had noticed some smoke from the oil later on, and came back and they cleaned it again right away even though the car had stopped smoking by the time I made it back.  These guys are on top of it when it comes to customer service.</review>

<Text>I couldn't wait to get into my new Mini. Those little cars are so cute and they're made by BMW - must be of good quality, or so I thought.
All the cars come with leather interiors and then there's the option for those sharp looking black enamel spoke wheels.  I ended up getting the Clubman model - it's more spacious than the Cooper and the ride is smoother.  I was happy with my little car ... for about 4 1/2 months, when it needed a brake pad replacement and, as it turned out, a front wheel alignment as well.
Not quite 6 months later, the brake pads needed replacement for the second time .... this is what I have to look forward to ??  I'm so regretful that I didn't go back to Honda - never had problems with those cars.
Honestly, in all my years of driving any make, style, used or new car,  I never had to have the brake pads replaced even once in less than a year.
When I questioned the service manager about the brake pads needing replacement so soon and so frequently, the answer I got was,
"Well, they're a sportier car so the brake pads tend to be a little softer."
Ok ... whatever.
I was also asked:
"Do you drive in a lot of stop and go traffic ?"
Really ??  (this is Los Angeles) Nah, not much.
I'm sorry but brake pads are absolutely essential for the safety of the driver, the passengers and, everyone else on the road.  How does a big name car manufacturer skimp on something as vital as brake pads and be okay with it ??
But if you're really bent on investing in one of those cute little Minis - PLEASE ! buy the extended warranty ... you're gonna need it !< /Text><rating>1< /rating>< user_name>
andrea lyn< /user_name>

March 4, 2016

On this time of regular check and repair of my BMW X-3
(at BMW of Monrovia, 1425-1451 South Mountain Ave. Monrovia, CA 91016)

This time of regular check was so far good as on the return drive from the service to my house.

But this time repair was very disappointed.
Reason is that both left and right LED rear tail light housings were replaced and charged $792.75 (including labor charge but not including tax).
When I visited at the service for the regular check and the repair, I told and requested the service person to do regular check and to fix only left rear light which was not turned on.
Then, the service person phoned and explained after they checked my X-3 that left rear LED light bulb itself was not be able to be replaced. Instead, whole assemble of rear LED light housings of not only left but also of right should be replaced.
I didn‚Äôt have any choice avoid this expensive and uncomfortable repair charge.

The points which I am very unhappy are ;

(1)	This time problem is definitely part defects (or parts not reliable). Current technology of LED light bulb is very reliable and long life. And These LED light whole housings are the original ones.  Why should I pay for it?
(2)	This LED housing design was not customer oriented. Because, Customers have to replace whole housing of both left and right instead of left LED light bulb it self. Why BMW (as one of the most honorable automobile manufacturer) had designed such customer uncomfortable one?

If you have any explanation of the reason why or any excuse against my points stated above, please send me an e-mail.
Also, if you refund the charge ($792.75), I am very comfortable.  Please let me know.

Noboru kasai
1641 Oakhaven Drive Arcadia CA, 91006</Review>
